  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_06251414-bdf2-4e11-8fdf-e88c47853507'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer7254050741646953391">When Gladiator Inc, an adult toy company expands their market to familiarize the ‘vanilla’ world with the elements of BDSM, the result is a pay-per-view reality show with video feeds streamed live to subscribers.   <span id="freeText7254050741646953391" style="display:none">When Gladiator Inc, an adult toy company expands their market to familiarize the ‘vanilla’ world with the elements of BDSM, the result is a pay-per-view reality show with video feeds streamed live to subscribers. The show, Dom Wars, is a competition to determine the Top Dom that will become the spokesperson for the company. <br /> <br />The contestants all wear cameras to film every moment and angle of the competition, while they complete various challenges to determine who has ultimately Dominated various elements of themselves. <br /> <br />The hero and heroine of the series, Lucian Bane and Tara Reese, have barely made it into the Sixth and Final Round of Dom Wars. This week-long Survival Round will determine the Top Dom, once and for all. <br /> <br />The contestants are taken to an uninhabited island, where they will have to cross formidable jungle terrain. First Dom to reach the boat anchored on the other side of the island wins the million dollars and the title. <br /> <br />Seems simple. Except Lucian’s old adversary, the Sadist Jase Duff from Round One, has been tasked with making sure none of the five teams make it to the boat. <br />If he is successful, he wins the prize, only it's not money that Jase Duff cares about, its revenge on Lucian and Tara. And his sadistic need to inflict pain makes it game on.</span>

<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/48615261-jules-tai"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1462075563i/48615261._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/48615261-jules-tai">Jules Tai</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I found this book to feel very different than the rest of the series. It got so much darker with all that was going on in the jungle...it suddenly bec<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I found this book to feel very different than the rest of the series. It got so much darker with all that was going on in the jungle...it suddenly became not only Dom Wars reality TV, but with Survivor thrown in (not that I've seen that). I think I actually like this book best in the series, it had me on edge for a good chunk of the book wondering what would happen next. <br /><br />I also really loved the camaraderie between Lucian, Tara, Preacher, and Becca. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1026104411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7743092730707373921"> It's over... I'm already in Dom Wars withdrawal, experiencing sub drop...<br/><br/>I was anticipating great things from this series ender and I wasn't disappointed. The authors came through in a big way with a host of twists and turns that kept the intensity level high throughout the entire book. There was no lack of explicit scenes and I loved the way the events of the game fueled Lucian's and Tara's mutual need for each other. The romance that has been developing over the last 5 books really blossomed </span>
  <span id="freeText7743092730707373921" style="display:none"> It's over... I'm already in Dom Wars withdrawal, experiencing sub drop...<br /><br />I was anticipating great things from this series ender and I wasn't disappointed. The authors came through in a big way with a host of twists and turns that kept the intensity level high throughout the entire book. There was no lack of explicit scenes and I loved the way the events of the game fueled Lucian's and Tara's mutual need for each other. The romance that has been developing over the last 5 books really blossomed in this one. The interaction between the characters in the book was tender and loving, but also showcased the unique D/s relationship that Lucian and Tara have - so elegant, respectful, and sweet. I did feel like the ending was a little abrupt. I wanted more warm and fuzzy as well as more about where the characters ended up, but I'm hopeful that these dedicated authors will have something down the road to help us with that closure.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7743092730707373921" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17233960693870997416" style="display:none">5 EPIC STARS!<br /> <br />THIS. IS. IT. <br />THE. FINAL. ROUND.<br /><br />I effing loved the final round. It was everything and nothing like I expected it to be. It was crazy, suspenseful, action packed, and had enough steam to make you sweat a bit. Ok and seriously, this book starts out with a bang making your kindle sizzle. I did not put this book down until the last word.<br /><br />This is the continuation of Lucian and Tara's story. This is it. With the tensions high, things are about to get crazy for these two. There will be twists and turns. They will experience ups and downs. But in the end, Tara and Lucian have one goal... make it to the finish line. Who will win the Dom Wars? Who will claim the one million dollars? And will they get the ultimate prize- forever?<br /><br />I have loved Lucian and Tara since Round One. I have loved their chemistry that has been building and building. I really thought this was the book we could their love shining through strongly. I loved how Lucian was the strong support for Tara and helped keep her focused. I also liked how much Tara grew from book one until the last. I also loved the family dynamics including Becca, Preacher, and Steve. Just an epic conclusion to an amazing series.<br /><br />I cannot wait to see what these two authors have in store for us next! :)<br /><br />Blog Tour---&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://reneeentress.blogspot.com/2014/08/blog-tour-review-giveaway-dom-wars.html">http://reneeentress.blogspot.com/2014...</a></span>

  <span id="freeText7489319591775845070" style="display:none">Holy shit! Pour yourself a glass of Kool-aid and get ready for the ride of your life. Lucian, Tara, Preacher Dom, and his wife, Becca are in the final round of Dom Wars. They get dropped into a remote jungle and are left to navigate their way through, having to get to designated areas laid out on a map to collect flags along the way. Then all they have to do is get to the beach, find and board the boat, and get off the island before the other competitors to be the winners. But dangers await them at every turn, whether they are animal, nature, or man-made, because running wild in the jungle with them, besides the other competitors, is Lucian’s old adversary that we first met in Dom Wars Round One, the evil sadist Jase Duff, and you will not believe the things he has been up to or how far he goes to keep Lucian and the group from finishing! This book was filled with suspense, romance, drama, and of course hot &amp; steamy sex! This book was as intense as the love is between Lucian and Tara. A total page-turner that I could not put down. A very satisfying ending to the Dom Wars series. </span>

It's like the authors didn't know what to do with the story line so they threw in a bunch of horrific violence to make it end. Plus they brought in these two other characters--Preacher mostly--and made him a key player. What about the great characters you started with? Why not explore their depths more and keep the dom wars about domination and submission instead of this absurd sidetrack off into reality TV BS. It's like it's not even the same author. Too bad.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1058237035" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1058237035" />
    <a title="Shanyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/794732-shanyn"><img alt="Shanyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392007588p2/794732.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1058237035?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shanyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shanyn" href="/user/show/794732-shanyn">Shanyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/794732-shanyn?shelf=favorite-characters">favorite-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/794732-shanyn?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1058237035" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer291461920961883596">Dom Wars has been an incredible journey. Not only for the characters in this incredible story, but for us as readers and for the author as well. When Lucian Bane blasted his way onto the indie book scene he brought with him a style and concept we hadn’t seen before. Telling a crazy hot love story that was overflowing with personality, suspense, intense personal demon domination, characters so real and honest that they crawled right under your skin and razor sharp humor. Each round has gathered s</span>
  <span id="freeText291461920961883596" style="display:none">Dom Wars has been an incredible journey. Not only for the characters in this incredible story, but for us as readers and for the author as well. When Lucian Bane blasted his way onto the indie book scene he brought with him a style and concept we hadn’t seen before. Telling a crazy hot love story that was overflowing with personality, suspense, intense personal demon domination, characters so real and honest that they crawled right under your skin and razor sharp humor. Each round has gathered speed until both book series and author have become one unstoppable force. <br /><br />Round 6 finds Lucian and Tara getting ready to head into an unknown island jungle with Preacher and Becca as they all struggle to just make it through this last hurdle before claiming the grand prize. Everything is even more unknown about this challenge than all of the others. They have no idea what they’re rappelling into other than danger and the unpredictable insanity that is Jase Duff who may or may not be laying in wait to kill them all. <br /><br />Watching these four characters traverse the jungle and all of its challenges was alternately hilarious, intensely suspenseful and creatively sexy. Preacher and Becca continue to work as the gorgeously tight knit team they are. And Lucian and Tara get even closer through their struggle as they come together to support each other through the unrelenting tension. By the end, all four of them work together as a well-oiled machine watching each other’s backs, complimenting their strengths expertly while compensating for their exhaustion and injuries effortlessly. <br /><br />The jungle becomes a character in and of itself almost overriding the humans in this installment. I sat on the edge of my seat never quite knowing what was going to come around the corner as the new threat. Not to mention the horror that is the sadist lurking in everyone’s peripheral vision. Suspense is absolutely the name of the game in this book. <br /><br />This is the first round in the series that Aden Lowe has co-written with Bane – although he’s been along for the whole ride as editor. The result is a gorgeously written book, laced through with nail-biting uncertainty built in an almost perfect arc. The tension is so beautifully constructed that I expected an equally explosive ending and it felt a bit rushed. But that tiny shadow in the spectacular landscape that is this book is hardly noticeable. <br /><br />The Dom Wars series will always stand alone in the erotica genre for its tone and scope. And while I am thrilled to see these characters through to their happy ending, I’m not even remotely happy to see it end. I’ve fallen in love with the perfect balance Bane has created between sex, humor and his brutally honest way of examining human nature. I’ve fallen in love with the cadence of his voice and the rhythm of his storytelling. How flayed open he leaves his characters and readers alike. <br /><br />I’m so glad that Lucian Bane is just getting warmed up. I’m so glad to know that this is just his beginning as an author. I know he has so much more to say and I’m looking forward to being the willing recipient to all of it. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="291461920961883596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8969295532797438051" style="display:none">I have totally fallen in love with this series and the characters Lucian has introduced us to. The struggles that Lucian and Tara have endured and conquered in Rounds 1 - 5 have been pretty amazing, but those pale in comparison to what the couple encounters in this final book! It is extremely intense!! Thankfully they are not alone. The Preacher and his lovely wife, Becca, whom we met in the previous book, are the perfect pair to undertake this challenge with. The setting couldn't possibly be any more hostile, an undeveloped tropical island with all of the "normal" hazards associated with the rainforest. Yuck! Add to that the danger of dealing with obstacles created by a completely insane enemy with a devious mindset. This round of Dom Wars requires that the couples not only work perfectly with each other, but they must also work cooperatively as a part of the larger team to accomplish the goal of traversing the island, gathering flags as they go, and being the first to finish. Authors Lucian Bane and Aden Lowe have masterfully created fascinating challenges and situations for this team to overcome!! Adding to the hardships, finding places and times in the jungle to act upon the fiery chemistry between Lucian and Tara is another challenge, and they learn to become quite resourceful in meeting that need!! And of course, as in the previous books, we expect to be treated to Lucian's quirky sense of humor and he comes through once again! <br /><br />The message of this series that has been present in all of the books, and it is the idea that dominance does not mean overpowering your partner in a way that weakens him/her. Dominance should always empower both parties and it is meant to be shared. These books have employed love and romance, humor, hot sex, and the unique format of competitive games to highlight Lucian's and Aden's message. I say "well done", and I'm excited for their next series, White Knight Academy! I highly recommend this series! </span>
  <a data-text-id="8969295532797438051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9189210253289813001">This is my 5 star review for Dom Wars Round Six by Lucian Bane and Aden Lowe.<br/>Dom Wars Round Six is the final round. Lucian, Tara, Preacher, and Becca are sent with the remaining teams to an unknown island with little survival items, a map, and a mad man chasing them.   <span id="freeText9189210253289813001" style="display:none">This is my 5 star review for Dom Wars Round Six by Lucian Bane and Aden Lowe.<br />Dom Wars Round Six is the final round. Lucian, Tara, Preacher, and Becca are sent with the remaining teams to an unknown island with little survival items, a map, and a mad man chasing them. Will they be able to complete their mission and make it out with one of them being named Top Dom? Will Jase Duff finally get to Lucian and tear his world apart?<br />This round was so much more than what I expected it to be. There was laughs, tears, and some HOT, oh my, moments as well. Lucian and Aden have a way with words. They show us just how much a man can love and protect the woman his heart desires. Round Six takes you on an island adventure you are sure to never forget. There are unforeseen plot twists and turns that had me on the edge of my seat. <br />I loved this whole series and this one was much different than the previous 5. Tara sure did show just how strong that she is in this one. She showed a strength and determination that I had not seen in previous books. Lucian showed us that it is okay to be scared and to fight for what we believe in. As always Steve was a hoot and Preacher started out being a big intimidation but ended up being one heck of a guy! I look forward to reading the new books that each author has planned for the future. I love their writing and their message! <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText15621439543338635975" style="display:none">When I first started reading this series, I had no ideal what to expect. I figured it would be some Doms fighting for something. This series has totally open my eyes to look at the Dom/sub relationship with new eyes. A lot of people might get the wrong ideal when they start this series especially if you have a preconceived view about what a Dom/sub relationship is.<br /><br />This series took me on a spiritual and eye opening ride. The more I read the more I saw that the Dom/sub relationship that Tara and Lucian had was more of what a Husband/wife relationship should be according to the bible. I'm sure everyone gets something different when they read this series but you REALLY should read it!<br /><br />Tara and Lucian find themselves in the round from hell. I loved the way this round kept me invested in what was happening. I was so tense I was so into it. The characters and story line held my attention and kept me engaged. This was a great series and I can't wait to see what is next from these two authors. Grab a copy and get reading.</span>

I have been a huge fan of the Dom Wars series and then the final round did a complete 360. The final book is some what like Survivor-ish book. I found it hard to read and it took me far more time to read it due to the disappointment. Then the abrupt ending. No, idea what happens after the final ceremony nothing! Sorry Lucian &amp; Aden!<br /><br />Round 6 is the final round and starts off dropping Tara, Lucian, Preacher &amp; Becca on an island to collect flags and cross the island to a boat and they win right? Hell effing no a big mind F is what I got. What happened to the intense passion, love, &amp; Gladiator activity? Because it wasn't in round 6. Action? Yes! But nothing like what we are accustomed to from the other rounds. I encourage you to purchase. Because if you are a Bane Train passenger you will want to know what happens. I warn you be prepared for the disappointment.<br /><br />Reviewed for Hooked On Books</span>

    <a title="Missy Fern - BFD Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17349469-missy-fern---bfd-book-blog"><img alt="Missy Fern - BFD Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455718090p2/17349469.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1030780296?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Missy Fern - BFD Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Missy Fern - BFD Book Blog" href="/user/show/17349469-missy-fern---bfd-book-blog">Missy Fern - BFD Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1030780296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13289794524964024038">This is the final round of Dom Wars. It's been great watching Tara and Lucian's love blossom under extreme circumstances. This book, however, was much different than the others because the story was really more about the competition and survival than Tara and Lucian' s relationship issues. An epilogue would have tied up loose ends for me....like what about the responsibilities Lucian took on for his subs (owes money), how/where Becca and Preacher end up, what Grandma thinks of Lucian, how/if the</span>
  <span id="freeText13289794524964024038" style="display:none">This is the final round of Dom Wars. It's been great watching Tara and Lucian's love blossom under extreme circumstances. This book, however, was much different than the others because the story was really more about the competition and survival than Tara and Lucian' s relationship issues. An epilogue would have tied up loose ends for me....like what about the responsibilities Lucian took on for his subs (owes money), how/where Becca and Preacher end up, what Grandma thinks of Lucian, how/if they deal with fame upon return to normal life, is there a baby on the way :) and wtf happened to Danielle. Therefore, consider this my request for Dom Wars 7.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13289794524964024038" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8882959822314876462" style="display:none"><strong>Dom Wars Final Round</strong><br /><br />In order to win the title of Top Dom contestants must propel into a private island/jungle, collect survival supplies, collect flags, and make it to an awaiting boat. <br />The Preacher and Becca chose to buy Lucian and Tara at the end of the previous round,making them a four man team. Who will be crowned the winner of a million dollars and title of Top Dom? Find out how this series ends! <br />***Needs to be read in order***<br />Great series Lucian Bane!!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14471103267569888053">Another home run for Mr. Bane! I have enjoyed this series from beginning to end. One long roller-coaster ride - but boy has it been thrilling.<br/><br/>Finally, the last round begins and this time things are a bit different. Tara, Lucian, Preacher and Becca are not just playing to win, they are playing to live - against a man who has a HUGE grudge and no problem killing in order to wreak vengeance on those he feels has wronged him.<br/><br/>I read this book in one fell swoop - couldn't put it down! <br/><br/>I look forward t</span>
  <span id="freeText14471103267569888053" style="display:none">Another home run for Mr. Bane! I have enjoyed this series from beginning to end. One long roller-coaster ride - but boy has it been thrilling.<br /><br />Finally, the last round begins and this time things are a bit different. Tara, Lucian, Preacher and Becca are not just playing to win, they are playing to live - against a man who has a HUGE grudge and no problem killing in order to wreak vengeance on those he feels has wronged him.<br /><br />I read this book in one fell swoop - couldn't put it down! <br /><br />I look forward to what Mr. Bane has in store for us in his future writing projects!<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16497059282126564064">Are you ready to be Dominated? <br/><br/>This is the final installment of the DOM WARS Series and it does not disappoint at all!! <br/>Lucian, Tara, Preacher, and Becca are sent with the remaining teams to an unknown island with little survival items, a map, and a mad man chasing them. Will they be able to complete their mission and make it out with one of them being named Top Dom? Will Jase Duff finally get to Lucian and tear his world apart?<br/><br/>With each round Lucian has just made me want more and I have to say </span>
  <span id="freeText16497059282126564064" style="display:none">Are you ready to be Dominated? <br /><br />This is the final installment of the DOM WARS Series and it does not disappoint at all!! <br />Lucian, Tara, Preacher, and Becca are sent with the remaining teams to an unknown island with little survival items, a map, and a mad man chasing them. Will they be able to complete their mission and make it out with one of them being named Top Dom? Will Jase Duff finally get to Lucian and tear his world apart?<br /><br />With each round Lucian has just made me want more and I have to say hands down that the final round is just an epic conclusion to an amazing series.<br /></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('P4Do/LdhDCi0JtCWnYu0h+0i1J9mGDCjhA0GmPeYYy16dAnYu0eU439bUepjxZtVZvFSdHh7oLjbFel+itGbGg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('giGDu8q+v0t5Osx4nFJm3irSn14qKg33hKRRJZtMPnvH1WKfxpgngLJHTQRiHEkMoQEZtTRJnezbvL7D5gXGTA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Being a Sinclair does have its perks. But things were simpler before the money. He may have been dirt poor, but he loved his job and fully intended to always come back from the sea to his girlfriend, Skye Weston, so they could move toward something more permanent. Or at least that had been the plan . . . until he returned from a two-month fishing trip to discover that she had moved away and was marrying somebody else. It tore his world apart.Now Skye’s back in town after nearly a decade. She’s a single mother and just as beautiful as ever. However, for some odd reason, she appears to hate him, when it should be Aiden who wants nothing to do with the woman who dumped him.
